1306 - </p><p>At level 80 <a href="/wiki/Summoning" title="Summoning">Summoning</a>, a player can use a <a href="/wiki/Hydra" title="Hydra">Hydra</a> familiar’s scroll to instantly regrow a tree grown in a farming patch, allowing for continuous chopping without competition from other players. This method results in a reasonable way to make money. The Patch in Gnome Stronghold should be used for this purpose as it's the closest to the bank. Other locations close to a bank would be the farming patch in Falador Park and the farming patch in the <a href="/wiki/Trahaearn" title="Trahaearn" class="mw-redirect">Trahaearn</a> section of <a href="/wiki/Prifddinas" title="Prifddinas">Prifddinas</a>.

8396 - </p><p>At level 80 <a href="/wiki/Summoning" title="Summoning">Summoning</a>, a player can use a <a href="/wiki/Hydra" title="Hydra">Hydra</a> familiar’s scroll to instantly regrow a tree grown in a farming patch, allowing for continuous chopping without competition from other players. This method results in a reasonable way to make money. The Patch in Gnome Stronghold should be used for this purpose as it's the closest to the bank. Other locations close to a bank would be the farming patch in Falador Park and the farming patch in the <a href="/wiki/Trahaearn" title="Trahaearn" class="mw-redirect">Trahaearn</a> section of <a href="/wiki/Prifddinas" title="Prifddinas">Prifddinas</a>.

13416 - </p>
13417 - </p><p>At level 80 <a href="/wiki/Summoning" title="Summoning">Summoning</a>, a player can use a <a href="/wiki/Hydra" title="Hydra">Hydra</a> familiar’s scroll to instantly regrow a tree grown in a farming patch, allowing for continuous chopping without competition from other players. This method results in a reasonable way to make money. The Patch in Gnome Stronghold should be used for this purpose as it's the closest to the bank. Other locations close to a bank would be the farming patch in Falador Park and the farming patch in the <a href="/wiki/Trahaearn" title="Trahaearn" class="mw-redirect">Trahaearn</a> section of <a href="/wiki/Prifddinas" title="Prifddinas">Prifddinas</a>.

37823 - </p><p>At level 80 <a href="/wiki/Summoning" title="Summoning">Summoning</a>, a player can use a <a href="/wiki/Hydra" title="Hydra">Hydra</a> familiar’s scroll to instantly regrow a tree grown in a farming patch, allowing for continuous chopping without competition from other players. This method results in a reasonable way to make money. The Patch in Gnome Stronghold should be used for this purpose as it's the closest to the bank. Other locations close to a bank would be the farming patch in Falador Park and the farming patch in the <a href="/wiki/Trahaearn" title="Trahaearn" class="mw-redirect">Trahaearn</a> section of <a href="/wiki/Prifddinas" title="Prifddinas">Prifddinas</a>.
